import random


def construction(trips):
    """ creates a list of tupples that indicate the time and strength of the trail [x,y]
    x being equal to the strength of the trail and direction, 1 being postive indicates trail 1 well negative indicates
    trail 2, y is equal to the time of the trail but moves down with each cycle of decay  
    """
    new_list = [] # Sets the list where the tupples will be added 
    totaltrips = 0  # Is a tally for the amount of trips the recurssive function undergos
    def construct_help(trips,new_list,totaltrips):
        prob = turn_prob(new_list) # Recalls what the new probability of the function is 
        choice = random.choice(range(0,100)) # Finds which way Ant feels like going
        print("__________Set ",totaltrips,"____________")
        print(choice,"Choice","|| Trip ", totaltrips)
        print(prob,"Prob")
        print(choice,"needs to be less than ", (prob[0]/(prob[0] + abs(prob[1]))) * 100, "for it to path 1")
        print("Probability of taking Path 1 is ", (prob[0]/(prob[0] + abs(prob[1]))))
        print( "Well Probability of taking Path 2 is ", (abs(prob[1])/(prob[0] + abs(prob[1])))) 
        if totaltrips == trips: #Ends the recursive call :(
            return new_list
        if choice <= (prob[0]/(prob[0] + abs(prob[1]))) * 100: # 50 decided by the comparison of path traveled
            new_list += [[5.00,totaltrips]] # constructed tupple in order to create decay observance
            #prob = turn_prob(decay(new_list)) Not sure if a decay function is necessary
            print(new_list)
            new_list = decaylinear(new_list)
            print(new_list)
            return construct_help(trips,new_list,totaltrips+1)
        else: 
        # if choice < (abs(prob[1])/(prob[0] + abs(prob[1])))*100 :
            new_list += [[-5.00,totaltrips]]
            #prob = turn_prob(decay(new_list)) 
            print(new_list)
            new_list = decaylinear(new_list)
            print(new_list)
            return construct_help(trips,new_list,totaltrips+1)   
    return construct_help(trips,new_list,totaltrips)

def decaylinear(n):
    new_list = []
    for x in range(0,len(n)):
        if n[x][1] == 0 or abs(n[x][0]) < .00000000000000001 or abs(n[x][0]) == 0 : # too be decided the value of "total diminish" 
            new_list = new_list
        if n[x][0] > 0:
            new_list += [[n[x][0]-.5,n[x][1]]]
        if n[x][0] < 0: 
            new_list += [[n[x][0]+.5,n[x][1]]]
    return new_list

def turn_prob(n):
    """ Calculates the turn probability of the"""
    negative_sum = -1
    postive_sum = 1
    if n == []:
        return (postive_sum,negative_sum)
    for x in range(0,len(n)-1):
        if  n[x][0] > 0:
            postive_sum += n[x][0]
        if n[x][0] < 0:
            negative_sum += n[x][0]
    return (postive_sum,negative_sum)      
def turn_increase(n):
    pass
